â˜•ï¸ Dining

1. Hotel breakfast variety and service (good or not): The excellence of catering is almost their biggest feature, and it is remarkable everywhere. ğŸŠ Hardware Facilities

1. Hotel environment: The fourth reason for liking this hotel is that it is too new. The hotel was soft-opened on December 31 last year and officially opened on March 31 this year. With several months of operational experience, the hotel is about to enter a colorful mature period. To be honest, the background of "hospitable Shandong" and its profound cultural heritage are particularly suitable for Huayu to be listed.
